\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01223}01223\ \ \ \ \ Checks\ X\ and\ y\ for\ consistent\ length,\ enforces\ X\ to\ be\ 2D\ and\ y\ 1D.\ By}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01224}01224\ \ \ \ \ default,\ X\ is\ checked\ to\ be\ non-\/empty\ and\ containing\ only\ finite\ values.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01225}01225\ \ \ \ \ Standard\ input\ checks\ are\ also\ applied\ to\ y,\ such\ as\ checking\ that\ y}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01226}01226\ \ \ \ \ does\ not\ have\ np.nan\ or\ np.inf\ targets.\ For\ multi-\/label\ y,\ set}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01227}01227\ \ \ \ \ multi\_output=True\ to\ allow\ 2D\ and\ sparse\ y.\ If\ the\ dtype\ of\ X\ is}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01228}01228\ \ \ \ \ object,\ attempt\ converting\ to\ float,\ raising\ on\ failure.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01559}01559\ \ \ \ \ symmetric.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01560}01560\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01955}\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesklearn_1_1utils_1_1validation_addb9557cb2e17288962287ce3c50e4d1}{01955}}\ def\ \_check\_psd\_eigenvalues(lambdas,\ enable\_warnings=False):}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01956}01956\ \ \ \ \ "{}"{}"{}Check\ the\ eigenvalues\ of\ a\ positive\ semidefinite\ (PSD)\ matrix.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01957}01957\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01958}01958\ \ \ \ \ Checks\ the\ provided\ array\ of\ PSD\ matrix\ eigenvalues\ for\ numerical\ or}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01959}01959\ \ \ \ \ conditioning\ issues\ and\ returns\ a\ fixed\ validated\ version.\ This\ method}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01960}01960\ \ \ \ \ should\ typically\ be\ used\ if\ the\ PSD\ matrix\ is\ user-\/provided\ (e.g.\ a}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01961}01961\ \ \ \ \ Gram\ matrix)\ or\ computed\ using\ a\ user-\/provided\ dissimilarity\ metric}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01962}01962\ \ \ \ \ (e.g.\ kernel\ function),\ or\ if\ the\ decomposition\ process\ uses\ approximation}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01963}01963\ \ \ \ \ methods\ (randomized\ SVD,\ etc.).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01964}01964\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01965}01965\ \ \ \ \ It\ checks\ for\ three\ things:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01966}01966\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01967}01967\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ that\ there\ are\ no\ significant\ imaginary\ parts\ in\ eigenvalues\ (more\ than}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01968}01968\ \ \ \ \ \ \ 1e-\/5\ times\ the\ maximum\ real\ part).\ If\ this\ check\ fails,\ it\ raises\ a}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01969}01969\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}ValueError\`{}\`{}.\ Otherwise\ all\ non-\/significant\ imaginary\ parts\ that\ may}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01970}01970\ \ \ \ \ \ \ remain\ are\ set\ to\ zero.\ This\ operation\ is\ traced\ with\ a}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01971}01971\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}PositiveSpectrumWarning\`{}\`{}\ when\ \`{}\`{}enable\_warnings=True\`{}\`{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01972}01972\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01973}01973\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ that\ eigenvalues\ are\ not\ all\ negative.\ If\ this\ check\ fails,\ it\ raises\ a}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01974}01974\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}ValueError\`{}\`{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01975}01975\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01976}01976\ \ \ \ \ -\/\ that\ there\ are\ no\ significant\ negative\ eigenvalues\ with\ absolute\ value}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01977}01977\ \ \ \ \ \ \ more\ than\ 1e-\/10\ (1e-\/6)\ and\ more\ than\ 1e-\/5\ (5e-\/3)\ times\ the\ largest}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01978}01978\ \ \ \ \ \ \ positive\ eigenvalue\ in\ double\ (simple)\ precision.\ If\ this\ check\ fails,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01979}01979\ \ \ \ \ \ \ it\ raises\ a\ \`{}\`{}ValueError\`{}\`{}.\ Otherwise\ all\ negative\ eigenvalues\ that\ may}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01980}01980\ \ \ \ \ \ \ remain\ are\ set\ to\ zero.\ This\ operation\ is\ traced\ with\ a}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01981}01981\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}PositiveSpectrumWarning\`{}\`{}\ when\ \`{}\`{}enable\_warnings=True\`{}\`{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01982}01982\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01983}01983\ \ \ \ \ Finally,\ all\ the\ positive\ eigenvalues\ that\ are\ too\ small\ (with\ a\ value}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01984}01984\ \ \ \ \ smaller\ than\ the\ maximum\ eigenvalue\ multiplied\ by\ 1e-\/12\ (2e-\/7))\ are\ set\ to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01985}01985\ \ \ \ \ zero.\ This\ operation\ is\ traced\ with\ a\ \`{}\`{}PositiveSpectrumWarning\`{}\`{}\ when}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01986}01986\ \ \ \ \ \`{}\`{}enable\_warnings=True\`{}\`{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01987}01987\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01988}01988\ \ \ \ \ Parameters}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01989}01989\ \ \ \ \ -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01995}01995\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ raised\ when\ there\ are\ imaginary\ parts,\ negative\ eigenvalues,\ or}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01996}01996\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ extremely\ small\ non-\/zero\ eigenvalues.\ Otherwise\ no\ warning\ will\ be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01997}01997\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ raised.\ In\ both\ cases,\ imaginary\ parts,\ negative\ eigenvalues,\ and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l01998}01998\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ extremely\ small\ non-\/zero\ eigenvalues\ will\ be\ set\ to\ zero.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l02051}02051\ \ \ \ \ \#\ Check\ that\ there\ are\ no\ significant\ imaginary\ parts}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l02052}02052\ \ \ \ \ if\ not\ np.isreal(lambdas).all():}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l02053}02053\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ max\_imag\_abs\ =\ np.abs(np.imag(lambdas)).max()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l02054}02054\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ max\_real\_abs\ =\ np.abs(np.real(lambdas)).max()}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l02087}02087\ \ \ \ \ else:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l02088}02088\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ min\_eig\ =\ lambdas.min()}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l02089}02089\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ if\ (}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l02090}02090\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ min\_eig\ <\ -\/significant\_neg\_ratio\ *\ max\_eig}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l02091}02091\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ and\ min\_eig\ <\ -\/significant\_neg\_value}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l02097}02097\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}the\ eigendecomposition\ of\ the\ matrix."{}\ \%\ (-\/min\_eig\ /\ max\_eig)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l02661}\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacesklearn_1_1utils_1_1validation_a199e87942398a6087bcf123d40b26e5a}{02661}}\ def\ \_to\_object\_array(sequence):}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l02662}02662\ \ \ \ \ "{}"{}"{}Convert\ sequence\ to\ a\ 1-\/D\ NumPy\ array\ of\ object\ dtype.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l02663}02663\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l02664}02664\ \ \ \ \ numpy.array\ constructor\ has\ a\ similar\ use\ but\ it's\ output}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l02665}02665\ \ \ \ \ is\ ambiguous.\ It\ can\ be\ 1-\/D\ NumPy\ array\ of\ object\ dtype\ if}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l02666}02666\ \ \ \ \ the\ input\ is\ a\ ragged\ array,\ but\ if\ the\ input\ is\ a\ list\ of}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l02667}02667\ \ \ \ \ equal\ length\ arrays,\ then\ the\ output\ is\ a\ 2D\ numpy.array.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l02668}02668\ \ \ \ \ \_to\_object\_array\ solves\ this\ ambiguity\ by\ guarantying\ that}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l02669}02669\ \ \ \ \ the\ output\ is\ a\ 1-\/D\ NumPy\ array\ of\ objects\ for\ any\ input.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{validation_8py_source_l02670}02670\ }
